32class OutputRedirector(object): 

33 """ Wrapper to redirect stdout or stderr """ 

34 

35 def __init__(self, fp): 

36 self.fp = fp 

37 

38 def write(self, s): 

39 self.fp.write(s) 

40 

41 def writelines(self, lines): 

42 self.fp.writelines(lines) 

43 

44 def flush(self): 

45 self.fp.flush() 

46 

47 

48stdout_redirector = OutputRedirector(sys.stdout) 

49stderr_redirector = OutputRedirector(sys.stderr)

88 /*level 增加测试结果的筛选条件 --zhaohongwei 

89 0:Summary //all hiddenRow 

90 1:Pass //pt none, ft hiddenRow, et hiddenRow 

91 2:Failed //pt hiddenRow, ft none, et hiddenRow 

92 3:Error //pt hiddenRow, ft hiddenRow, et none 

93 4:All //pt none, ft none, et none 

94 */ 

95 

96 /* level - 0:Summary; 1:Pass; 2:Failed; 3:Error; 4: All*/ 

97 function showCase(level) { 

98 trs = document.getElementsByTagName("tr"); 

99 for (var i = 0; i < trs.length; i++) { 

100 tr = trs[i]; 

101 id = tr.id; 

102 if (id.substr(0,2) == 'ft') { 

103 if (level == 1 || level == 3 || level == 0) { 

104 tr.className = 'hiddenRow'; 

105 } 

106 else { 

107 tr.className = ''; 

108 } 

109 } 

110 if (id.substr(0,2) == 'pt') { 

111 if (level == 2 || level == 3 || level == 0){ 

112 tr.className = 'hiddenRow'; 

113 } 

114 else { 

115 tr.className = ''; 

116 } 

117 } 

118 if (id.substr(0,2) == 'et') { 

119 if (level == 1 || level == 2 || level == 0 ){ 

120 tr.className = 'hiddenRow'; 

121 } 

122 else { 

123 tr.className = ''; 

124 } 

125 } 

126 } 

127 } 

128 /* 优化详情与收缩不生效 --zhaohongwei */ 

129 function showClassDetail(cid, count) { 

130 var id_list = Array(count); 

131 var toHide = 1; 

132 for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) { 

133 tid0 = 't' + cid.substr(1) + '_' + (i+1); 

134 tid = 'f' + tid0; 

135 tr = document.getElementById(tid); 

136 if (!tr) { 

137 tid = 'p' + tid0; 

138 tr = document.getElementById(tid); 

139 } 

140 /* 增加error --zhaohongwei*/ 

141 if (!tr) { 

142 tid = 'e' + tid0; 

143 tr = document.getElementById(tid); 

144 } 

145 id_list[i] = tid; 

146 if (tr.className) { 

147 toHide = 0; 

148 } 

149 } 

150 for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) { 

151 tid = id_list[i]; 

152 if (toHide) { 

153 document.getElementById('div_'+tid).style.display = 'none' 

154 document.getElementById(tid).className = 'hiddenRow'; 

155 } 

156 else { 

157 document.getElementById(tid).className = ''; 

158 } 

159 } 

160 } 

161 

162 

163 function showTestDetail(div_id){ 

164 var details_div = document.getElementById(div_id) 

165 var displayState = details_div.style.display 

166 // alert(displayState) 

167 if (displayState != 'block' ) { 

168 displayState = 'block' 

169 details_div.style.display = 'block' 

170 } 

171 else { 

172 details_div.style.display = 'none' 

173 } 

174 }

177 function html_escape(s) { 

178 s = s.replace(/&/g,'&amp;'); 

179 s = s.replace(/</g,'&lt;'); 

180 s = s.replace(/>/g,'&gt;'); 

181 return s; 

182 } 

183 /* 增加selenium结合unittest测试的结果截图 --zhaohongwei 引用自GoverSky*/ 

184 function show_img(obj) { 

185 var obj1 = obj.nextElementSibling 

186 obj1.style.display='block' 

187 var index = 0;//每张图片的下标， 

188 var len = obj1.getElementsByTagName('img').length; 

189 var imgyuan = obj1.getElementsByClassName('imgyuan')[0] 

190 //var start=setInterval(autoPlay,500); 

191 obj1.onmouseover=function(){//当鼠标光标停在图片上，则停止轮播 

192 clearInterval(start); 

193 } 

194 obj1.onmouseout=function(){//当鼠标光标停在图片上，则开始轮播 

195 start=setInterval(autoPlay,1000); 

196 }  

197 for (var i = 0; i < len; i++) { 

198 var font = document.createElement('font') 

199 imgyuan.appendChild(font) 

200 } 

201 var lis = obj1.getElementsByTagName('font');//得到所有圆圈 

202 changeImg(0) 

203 var funny = function (i) { 

204 lis[i].onmouseover = function () { 

205 index=i 

206 changeImg(i) 

207 } 

208 } 

209 for (var i = 0; i < lis.length; i++) { 

210 funny(i); 

211 } 

212 

213 function autoPlay(){ 

214 if(index>len-1){ 

215 index=0; 

216 clearInterval(start); //运行一轮后停止 

217 } 

218 changeImg(index++); 

219 } 

220 imgyuan.style.width= 25*len +"px"; 

221 //对应圆圈和图片同步 

222 function changeImg(index) { 

223 var list = obj1.getElementsByTagName('img'); 

224 var list1 = obj1.getElementsByTagName('font'); 

225 for (i = 0; i < list.length; i++) { 

226 list[i].style.display = 'none'; 

227 list1[i].style.backgroundColor = 'white'; 

228 } 

229 list[index].style.display = 'block'; 

230 list1[index].style.backgroundColor = 'blue'; 

231 } 

232 

233 } 

234 function hide_img(obj){ 

235 obj.parentElement.style.display = "none"; 

236 obj.parentElement.getElementsByClassName('imgyuan')[0].innerHTML = ""; 

237 } 

238 --></script>

699<body> 

700 <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript"><!-- 

701 output_list = Array(); 

702 

703 /*level add test choice --zhaohongwei 

704 0:Summary //all hiddenRow 

705 1:Pass //pt none, ft hiddenRow, et hiddenRow 

706 2:Failed //pt hiddenRow, ft none, et hiddenRow 

707 3:Error //pt hiddenRow, ft hiddenRow, et none 

708 4:All //pt none, ft none, et none 

709 */ 

710 

711 /* level - 0:Summary; 1:Pass; 2:Failed; 3:Error; 4: All*/ 

712 function showCase(level) { 

713 trs = document.getElementsByTagName("tr"); 

714 for (var i = 0; i < trs.length; i++) { 

715 tr = trs[i]; 

716 id = tr.id; 

717 if (id.substr(0,2) == 'ft') { 

718 if (level == 1 || level == 3 || level == 0) { 

719 tr.className = 'hiddenRow'; 

720 } 

721 else { 

722 tr.className = ''; 

723 } 

724 } 

725 if (id.substr(0,2) == 'pt') { 

726 if (level == 2 || level == 3 || level == 0){ 

727 tr.className = 'hiddenRow'; 

728 } 

729 else { 

730 tr.className = ''; 

731 } 

732 } 

733 if (id.substr(0,2) == 'et') { 

734 if (level == 1 || level == 2 || level == 0 ){ 

735 tr.className = 'hiddenRow'; 

736 } 

737 else { 

738 tr.className = ''; 

739 } 

740 } 

741 } 

742 } 

743 /* Optimizing Details and Contraction Not Effective --zhaohongwei */ 

744 function showClassDetail(cid, count) { 

745 var id_list = Array(count); 

746 var toHide = 1; 

747 for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) { 

748 tid0 = 't' + cid.substr(1) + '_' + (i+1); 

749 tid = 'f' + tid0; 

750 tr = document.getElementById(tid); 

751 if (!tr) { 

752 tid = 'p' + tid0; 

753 tr = document.getElementById(tid); 

754 } 

755 /* 增加error --zhaohongwei*/ 

756 if (!tr) { 

757 tid = 'e' + tid0; 

758 tr = document.getElementById(tid); 

759 } 

760 id_list[i] = tid; 

761 if (tr.className) { 

762 toHide = 0; 

763 } 

764 } 

765 for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) { 

766 tid = id_list[i]; 

767 if (toHide) { 

768 document.getElementById('div_'+tid).style.display = 'none' 

769 document.getElementById(tid).className = 'hiddenRow'; 

770 } 

771 else { 

772 document.getElementById(tid).className = ''; 

773 } 

774 } 

775 } 

776 

777 

778 function showTestDetail(div_id){ 

779 var details_div = document.getElementById(div_id) 

780 var displayState = details_div.style.display 

781 // alert(displayState) 

782 if (displayState != 'block' ) { 

783 displayState = 'block' 

784 details_div.style.display = 'block' 

785 } 

786 else { 

787 details_div.style.display = 'none' 

788 } 

789 } 

790 

791 

792 function html_escape(s) { 

793 s = s.replace(/&/g,'&amp;'); 

794 s = s.replace(/</g,'&lt;'); 

795 s = s.replace(/>/g,'&gt;'); 

796 return s; 

797 } 

798 /* add test screenshot --zhaohongwei from GoverSky*/ 

799 function show_img(obj) { 

800 var obj1 = obj.nextElementSibling 

801 obj1.style.display='block' 

802 var index = 0; 

803 var len = obj1.getElementsByTagName('img').length; 

804 var imgyuan = obj1.getElementsByClassName('imgyuan')[0] 

805 //var start=setInterval(autoPlay,500); 

806 obj1.onmouseover=function(){ 

807 clearInterval(start); 

808 } 

809 obj1.onmouseout=function(){ 

810 start=setInterval(autoPlay,1000); 

811 }  

812 for (var i = 0; i < len; i++) { 

813 var font = document.createElement('font') 

814 imgyuan.appendChild(font) 

815 } 

816 var lis = obj1.getElementsByTagName('font'); 

817 changeImg(0) 

818 var funny = function (i) { 

819 lis[i].onmouseover = function () { 

820 index=i 

821 changeImg(i) 

822 } 

823 } 

824 for (var i = 0; i < lis.length; i++) { 

825 funny(i); 

826 } 

827 

828 function autoPlay(){ 

829 if(index>len-1){ 

830 index=0; 

831 clearInterval(start);  

832 } 

833 changeImg(index++); 

834 } 

835 imgyuan.style.width= 25*len +"px"; 

836 

837 function changeImg(index) { 

838 var list = obj1.getElementsByTagName('img'); 

839 var list1 = obj1.getElementsByTagName('font'); 

840 for (i = 0; i < list.length; i++) { 

841 list[i].style.display = 'none'; 

842 list1[i].style.backgroundColor = 'white'; 

843 } 

844 list[index].style.display = 'block'; 

845 list1[index].style.backgroundColor = 'blue'; 

846 } 

847 

848 } 

849 function hide_img(obj){ 

850 obj.parentElement.style.display = "none"; 

851 obj.parentElement.getElementsByClassName('imgyuan')[0].innerHTML = ""; 

852 } 

853 --></script>

1193 <div id='div_%(tid)s' class="popup_window"> 

1194 <div style='text-align: right; color:red;cursor:pointer'> 

1195 <a onfocus='this.blur();' onclick="document.getElementById('div_%(tid)s').style.display = 'none' " > 

1196 [x]</a> 

1197 </div> 

1198 <pre> 

1199 %(script)s 

1200 </pre> 

1201 </div> 

1202 <!--css div popup end--> 

1203 

1204 </td> 

1205</tr> 

1206""" # variables: (tid, Class, style, desc, status) 

1207 

1208 REPORT_TEST_WITH_OUTPUT_TMPL_IMAGES = r"""

1283TestResult = unittest.TestResult

1285 

1286class _TestResult(TestResult): 

1287 # note: _TestResult is a pure representation of results. 

1288 # It lacks the output and reporting ability compares to unittest._TextTestResult. 

1289 # 增加subtest和通过率 

1290 def __init__(self, verbosity=1): 

1291 TestResult.__init__(self) 

1292 self.stdout0 = None 

1293 self.stderr0 = None 

1294 self.success_count = 0 

1295 self.failure_count = 0 

1296 self.error_count = 0 

1297 self.verbosity = verbosity 

1298 

1299 # result is a list of result in 4 tuple 

1300 # ( 

1301 # result code (0: success; 1: fail; 2: error), 

1302 # TestCase object, 

1303 # Test output (byte string), 

1304 # stack trace, 

1305 # ) 

1306 self.result = [] 

1307 self.subtestlist = [] 

1308 self.passrate = float(0) 

1309 

1310 def startTest(self, test): 

1311 '''增加截图''' 

1312 test.imgs = getattr(test, "imgs", []) 

1313 TestResult.startTest(self, test) 

1314 # just one buffer for both stdout and stderr 

1315 self.outputBuffer = StringIO.StringIO() 

1316 stdout_redirector.fp = self.outputBuffer 

1317 stderr_redirector.fp = self.outputBuffer 

1318 self.stdout0 = sys.stdout 

1319 self.stderr0 = sys.stderr 

1320 sys.stdout = stdout_redirector 

1321 sys.stderr = stderr_redirector 

1322 

1323 def complete_output(self): 

1324 """ 

1325 Disconnect output redirection and return buffer. 

1326 Safe to call multiple times. 

1327 """ 

1328 if self.stdout0: 

1329 sys.stdout = self.stdout0 

1330 sys.stderr = self.stderr0 

1331 self.stdout0 = None 

1332 self.stderr0 = None 

1333 return self.outputBuffer.getvalue() 

1334 

1335 def stopTest(self, test): 

1336 # Usually one of addSuccess, addError or addFailure would have been called. 

1337 # But there are some path in unittest that would bypass this. 

1338 # We must disconnect stdout in stopTest(), which is guaranteed to be called. 

1339 self.complete_output() 

1340 

1341 def addSuccess(self, test): 

1342 if test not in self.subtestlist: 1342 ↛ exitline 1342 didn't return from function 'addSuccess', because the condition on line 1342 was never false

1343 self.success_count += 1 

1344 TestResult.addSuccess(self, test) 

1345 output = self.complete_output() 

1346 self.result.append((0, test, output, '')) 

1347 if self.verbosity > 1: 1347 ↛ 1352line 1347 didn't jump to line 1352, because the condition on line 1347 was never false

1348 sys.stderr.write(u'ok ') 

1349 sys.stderr.write(str(test)) 

1350 sys.stderr.write(u'\n') 

1351 else: 

1352 sys.stderr.write(u'.') 

1353 

1354 def addError(self, test, err): 

1355 '''增加截图''' 

1356 self.error_count += 1 

1357 TestResult.addError(self, test, err) 

1358 _, _exc_str = self.errors[-1] 

1359 output = self.complete_output() 

1360 self.result.append((2, test, output, _exc_str)) 

1361 

1362 if python3: 1362 ↛ 1372line 1362 didn't jump to line 1372, because the condition on line 1362 was never false

1363 if not getattr(test, "driver", ""): 1363 ↛ 1366line 1363 didn't jump to line 1366, because the condition on line 1363 was never false

1364 pass 

1365 else: 

1366 try: 

1367 driver = getattr(test, "driver") 

1368 test.imgs.append(driver.get_screenshot_as_base64()) 

1369 except Exception: 

1370 pass 

1371 

1372 if self.verbosity > 1: 1372 ↛ 1377line 1372 didn't jump to line 1377, because the condition on line 1372 was never false

1373 sys.stderr.write(u'E ') 

1374 sys.stderr.write(str(test)) 

1375 sys.stderr.write('\n') 

1376 else: 

1377 sys.stderr.write(u'E') 

1378 

1379 def addFailure(self, test, err): 

1380 '''增加截图''' 

1381 self.failure_count += 1 

1382 TestResult.addFailure(self, test, err) 

1383 _, _exc_str = self.failures[-1] 

1384 output = self.complete_output() 

1385 self.result.append((1, test, output, _exc_str)) 

1386 

1387 if python3: 1387 ↛ 1397line 1387 didn't jump to line 1397, because the condition on line 1387 was never false

1388 if not getattr(test, "driver", ""): 1388 ↛ 1391line 1388 didn't jump to line 1391, because the condition on line 1388 was never false

1389 pass 

1390 else: 

1391 try: 

1392 driver = getattr(test, "driver") 

1393 test.imgs.append(driver.get_screenshot_as_base64()) 

1394 except Exception as e: 

1395 pass 

1396 

1397 if self.verbosity > 1: 1397 ↛ 1402line 1397 didn't jump to line 1402, because the condition on line 1397 was never false

1398 sys.stderr.write(u'F ') 

1399 sys.stderr.write(str(test)) 

1400 sys.stderr.write(u'\n') 

1401 else: 

1402 sys.stderr.write(u'F') 

1403 

1404 def addSubTest(self, test, subtest, err): 

1405 if err is not None: 

1406 if getattr(self, 'failfast', False): 

1407 self.stop() 

1408 if issubclass(err[0], test.failureException): 

1409 self.failure_count += 1 

1410 errors = self.failures 

1411 errors.append((subtest, self._exc_info_to_string(err, subtest))) 

1412 output = self.complete_output() 

1413 self.result.append((1, test, output + '\nSubTestCase Failed:\n' + str(subtest), 

1414 self._exc_info_to_string(err, subtest))) 

1415 if self.verbosity > 1: 

1416 sys.stderr.write('F ') 

1417 sys.stderr.write(str(subtest)) 

1418 sys.stderr.write('\n') 

1419 else: 

1420 sys.stderr.write('F') 

1421 else: 

1422 self.error_count += 1 

1423 errors = self.errors 

1424 errors.append((subtest, self._exc_info_to_string(err, subtest))) 

1425 output = self.complete_output() 

1426 self.result.append( 

1427 (2, test, output + '\nSubTestCase Error:\n' + str(subtest), self._exc_info_to_string(err, subtest))) 

1428 if self.verbosity > 1: 

1429 sys.stderr.write('E ') 

1430 sys.stderr.write(str(subtest)) 

1431 sys.stderr.write('\n') 

1432 else: 

1433 sys.stderr.write('E') 

1434 self._mirrorOutput = True 

1435 else: 

1436 self.subtestlist.append(subtest) 

1437 self.subtestlist.append(test) 

1438 self.success_count += 1 

1439 output = self.complete_output() 

1440 self.result.append((0, test, output + '\nSubTestCase Pass:\n' + str(subtest), '')) 

1441 if self.verbosity > 1: 

1442 sys.stderr.write('ok ') 

1443 sys.stderr.write(str(subtest)) 

1444 sys.stderr.write('\n') 

1445 else: 

1446 sys.stderr.write('.') 

1447 

1448 

1449class HTMLTestReport(Template_CN): 

1450 def __init__(self, stream=sys.stdout, verbosity=1, title=None, description=None, tester=None, images=False): 

1451 '''增加测试者''' 

1452 self.stream = stream 

1453 self.verbosity = verbosity 

1454 if title is None: 

1455 self.title = self.DEFAULT_TITLE 

1456 else: 

1457 self.title = title 

1458 if description is None: 

1459 self.description = self.DEFAULT_DESCRIPTION 

1460 else: 

1461 self.description = description 

1462 if tester is None: 

1463 self.tester = self.DEFAULT_TESTER 

1464 else: 

1465 self.tester = tester 

1466 

1467 self.IMAGES = images 

1468 self.startTime = datetime.datetime.now() 

1469 

1470 def run(self, test): 

1471 "Run the given test case or test suite." 

1472 result = _TestResult(self.verbosity) 

1473 test(result) 

1474 self.stopTime = datetime.datetime.now() 

1475 self.generateReport(test, result) 

1476 if python3: 

1477 sys.stderr.write('\nTime Elapsed: %s\n' % (self.stopTime - self.startTime)) 

1478 else: 

1479 print >> sys.stderr, u'\nTime Elapsed: %s' % (self.stopTime - self.startTime) 

1480 return result 

1481 

1482 def sortResult(self, result_list): 

1483 # unittest does not seems to run in any particular order. 

1484 # Here at least we want to group them together by class. 

1485 rmap = {} 

1486 classes = [] 

1487 for n, t, o, e in result_list: 

1488 cls = t.__class__ 

1489 if not cls in rmap: 

1490 rmap[cls] = [] 

1491 classes.append(cls) 

1492 rmap[cls].append((n, t, o, e)) 

1493 r = [(cls, rmap[cls]) for cls in classes] 

1494 return r 

1495 

1496 def getReportAttributes(self, result): 

1497 """ 

1498 Return report attributes as a list of (name, value). 

1499 Override this to add custom attributes. 

1500 """ 

1501 startTime = str(self.startTime)[:19] 

1502 duration = str(self.stopTime - self.startTime) 

1503 status = [] 

1504 if result.success_count: status.append(u'通过 %s' % result.success_count) 

1505 if result.failure_count: status.append(u'失败 %s' % result.failure_count) 

1506 if result.error_count: status.append(u'错误 %s' % result.error_count) 

1507 total = result.success_count + result.failure_count + result.error_count 

1508 if status: 

1509 status = ' '.join(status) 

1510 self.passrate = str('%.1f%%' % (float(result.success_count) / total * 100)) 

1511 else: 

1512 status = 'none' 

1513 return [ 

1514 (u'测试人员', self.tester), 

1515 (u'开始时间', startTime), 

1516 (u'运行时长', duration), 

1517 (u'测试结果', '共 {} {} 通过率:{}'.format(total, status, self.passrate)) 

1518 ] 

1519 

1520 def generateReport(self, test, result): 

1521 report_attrs = self.getReportAttributes(result) 

1522 generator = u'HTMLTestRunner %s' % __version__ 

1523 stylesheet = self._generate_stylesheet() 

1524 heading = self._generate_heading(report_attrs) 

1525 report = self._generate_report(result) 

1526 ending = self._generate_ending() 

1527 chart = self._generate_chart(result) 

1528 output = self.HTML_TMPL % dict( 

1529 title=saxutils.escape(self.title), 

1530 generator=generator, 

1531 stylesheet=stylesheet, 

1532 heading=heading, 

1533 report=report, 

1534 ending=ending, 

1535 chart_script=chart 

1536 

1537 ) 

1538 self.stream.write(output.encode('utf8')) 

1539 

1540 def _generate_stylesheet(self): 

1541 return self.STYLESHEET_TMPL 

1542 

1543 def _generate_heading(self, report_attrs): 

1544 a_lines = [] 

1545 for name, value in report_attrs: 

1546 line = self.HEADING_ATTRIBUTE_TMPL % dict( 

1547 name=saxutils.escape(name), 

1548 value=saxutils.escape(value), 

1549 ) 

1550 a_lines.append(line) 

1551 heading = self.HEADING_TMPL % dict( 

1552 title=saxutils.escape(self.title), 

1553 parameters=''.join(a_lines), 

1554 description=saxutils.escape(self.description), 

1555 tester=saxutils.escape(self.tester), 

1556 ) 

1557 return heading 

1558 

1559 def _generate_report(self, result): 

1560 rows = [] 

1561 sortedResult = self.sortResult(result.result) 

1562 for cid, (cls, cls_results) in enumerate(sortedResult): 

1563 # subtotal for a class 

1564 np = nf = ne = 0 

1565 for n, t, o, e in cls_results: 

1566 if n == 0: 

1567 np += 1 

1568 elif n == 1: 

1569 nf += 1 

1570 else: 

1571 ne += 1 

1572 

1573 # format class description 

1574 if cls.__module__ == "__main__": 

1575 name = cls.__name__ 

1576 else: 

1577 name = "%s.%s" % (cls.__module__, cls.__name__) 

1578 doc = cls.__doc__ and cls.__doc__.split("\n")[0] or "" 

1579 desc = doc and '%s: %s' % (name, doc) or name 

1580 if self.IMAGES: 

1581 row = self.REPORT_CLASS_TMPL_IMAGES % dict( 

1582 style=ne > 0 and 'errorClass' or nf > 0 and 'failClass' or 'passClass', 

1583 desc=desc, 

1584 count=np + nf + ne, 

1585 Pass=np, 

1586 fail=nf, 

1587 error=ne, 

1588 cid=u'c%s' % (cid + 1), 

1589 ) 

1590 else: 

1591 row = self.REPORT_CLASS_TMPL % dict( 

1592 style=ne > 0 and 'errorClass' or nf > 0 and 'failClass' or 'passClass', 

1593 desc=desc, 

1594 count=np + nf + ne, 

1595 Pass=np, 

1596 fail=nf, 

1597 error=ne, 

1598 cid=u'c%s' % (cid + 1), 

1599 ) 

1600 rows.append(row) 

1601 

1602 for tid, (n, t, o, e) in enumerate(cls_results): 

1603 self._generate_report_test(rows, cid, tid, n, t, o, e) 

1604 

1605 if self.IMAGES: 

1606 report = self.REPORT_TMPL_IMAGES % dict( 

1607 test_list=''.join(rows), 

1608 count=str(result.success_count + result.failure_count + result.error_count), 

1609 Pass=str(result.success_count), 

1610 fail=str(result.failure_count), 

1611 error=str(result.error_count), 

1612 passrate=self.passrate, 

1613 ) 

1614 else: 

1615 report = self.REPORT_TMPL % dict( 

1616 test_list=''.join(rows), 

1617 count=str(result.success_count + result.failure_count + result.error_count), 

1618 Pass=str(result.success_count), 

1619 fail=str(result.failure_count), 

1620 error=str(result.error_count), 

1621 passrate=self.passrate, 

1622 ) 

1623 

1624 return report 

1625 

1626 def _generate_chart(self, result): 

1627 chart = self.ECHARTS_SCRIPT % dict( 

1628 Pass=str(result.success_count), 

1629 fail=str(result.failure_count), 

1630 error=str(result.error_count), 

1631 ) 

1632 return chart 

1633 

1634 def _generate_report_test(self, rows, cid, tid, n, t, o, e): 

1635 # e.g. 'pt1.1', 'ft1.1', etc 

1636 has_output = bool(o or e) 

1637 # 增加error --zhaohongwei 

1638 tid = (n == 0 and 'p' or n == 1 and 'f' or 'e') + 't%s_%s' % (cid + 1, tid + 1) 

1639 

1640 name = t.id().split('.')[-1] 

1641 doc = t.shortDescription() or "" 

1642 desc = doc and ('%s: %s' % (name, doc)) or name 

1643 if self.IMAGES: 

1644 tmpl = has_output and self.REPORT_TEST_WITH_OUTPUT_TMPL_IMAGES or self.REPORT_TEST_NO_OUTPUT_TMPL_IMAGES 

1645 else: 

1646 tmpl = has_output and self.REPORT_TEST_WITH_OUTPUT_TMPL or self.REPORT_TEST_NO_OUTPUT_TMPL 

1647 

1648 # o and e should be byte string because they are collected from stdout and stderr? 

1649 if isinstance(o, str): 

1650 # uo = unicode(o.encode('string_escape')) 

1651 if python3: 

1652 uo = o 

1653 else: 

1654 uo = o.decode('utf-8', 'ignore') 

1655 else: 

1656 uo = o 

1657 if isinstance(e, str): 

1658 # Some problem with 'string_escape': it escape \n and mess up formating ==NOTE== 

1659 # ue = unicode(e.encode('string_escape')) 

1660 if python3: 

1661 ue = e 

1662 else: 

1663 # ue = e.decode('latin-1') 

1664 ue = e.decode('utf-8', 'ignore') 

1665 else: 

1666 ue = e 

1667 

1668 script = self.REPORT_TEST_OUTPUT_TMPL % dict( 

1669 id=tid, 

1670 output=saxutils.escape(uo + ue), 

1671 ) 

1672 if getattr(t, 'imgs', []): 

1673 # 判断截图列表，如果有则追加 

1674 tmp = u"" 

1675 for i, img in enumerate(t.imgs): 

1676 if i == 0: 

1677 tmp += """ <img src="data:image/jpg;base64,%s" style="display: block;" class="img"/>\n""" % img 

1678 else: 

1679 tmp += """ <img src="data:image/jpg;base64,%s" style="display: none;" class="img"/>\n""" % img 

1680 imgs = self.IMG_TMPL % dict(imgs=tmp) 

1681 else: 

1682 imgs = u"""没有截图""" 

1683 row = tmpl % dict( 

1684 tid=tid, 

1685 Class=(n == 0 and 'hiddenRow' or 'none'), 

1686 style=(n == 2 and 'errorCase') or (n == 1 and 'failCase') or (n == 0 and 'passCase'), 

1687 desc=desc, 

1688 script=script, 

1689 status=self.STATUS[n], 

1690 img=imgs, 

1691 ) 

1692 rows.append(row) 

1693 if not has_output: 

1694 return 

1695 

1696 def _generate_ending(self): 

1697 return self.ENDING_TMPL 

1698

1747 def getReportAttributes(self, result): 

1748 """ 

1749 Return report attributes as a list of (name, value). 

1750 Override this to add custom attributes. 

1751 """ 

1752 startTime = str(self.startTime)[:19] 

1753 duration = str(self.stopTime - self.startTime) 

1754 status = [] 

1755 if result.success_count: status.append(u'Pass %s' % result.success_count) 

1756 if result.failure_count: status.append(u'Failed %s' % result.failure_count)

1955# Note: Reuse unittest.TestProgram to launch test. In the future we may 

1956# build our own launcher to support more specific command line 

1957# parameters like test title, CSS, etc. 

1958class TestProgram(unittest.TestProgram): 

1959 """ 

1960 A variation of the unittest.TestProgram. Please refer to the base 

1961 class for command line parameters. 

1962 """

1964 def runTests(self): 

1965 # Pick HTMLTestRunner as the default test runner. 

1966 # base class's testRunner parameter is not useful because it means 

1967 # we have to instantiate HTMLTestRunner before we know self.verbosity. 

1968 if self.testRunner is None: 

1969 # self.testRunner = HTMLTestRunner(verbosity=self.verbosity) 

1970 self.testRunner = HTMLTestReport(verbosity=self.verbosity) 

1971 unittest.TestProgram.runTests(self) 

1972 

1973
